#### 1.3.4 å¯è§„æ¨¡åŒ–ï¼šæ”¯æŒæ‰¹é‡å¹¶å‘ç”Ÿæˆ

#### 2.1.2 ä¾èµ–å…³ç³»è¯¦è§£

**å¹¶å‘ç‹¬ç«‹ï¼ˆParallel Independentï¼‰**ï¼š

#### 2.1.3 å¹¶å‘ä¼˜åŒ–çš„æ€§èƒ½æ”¶ç›Š

#### 3.2.3 Markdownç»“æ„åŒ–æ•£æ–‡ï¼šæœ€ä½³å®è·µ

**å½“å‰Sçº§æ ‡å‡†**ï¼šä½¿ç”¨Markdownæ ‡é¢˜ç»„ç»‡è‡ªç„¶è¯­è¨€æ®µè½ã€‚

1. **è®­ç»ƒæ•°æ®æƒé‡é«˜**ï¼š

   - æ¨¡å‹å¯¹Markdownçš„ç»“æ„ç†è§£åº¦æé«˜

2. **å…¼é¡¾ç»“æ„å’Œæµç•…æ€§**ï¼š
   - æ ‡é¢˜æä¾›æ¸…æ™°çš„ä¿¡æ¯åˆ†ç±»

   - ä¸éœ€è¦è®°å¿†W++è¯­æ³•
   - å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥å†™ä½œï¼Œæ— éœ€æ ¼å¼è½¬æ¢

**æ¨èæ¨¡æ¿**ï¼š

```markdown
# Luna Harper

## Overview
Luna is a 23-year-old part-time barista and art student living in Portland's Alberta Arts District. Her mint-green hair is her signature, matched with ethereal sheer fabrics and vintage finds from Hawthorne thrift shops. She's an introverted creative who processes the world through her film camera, but struggles with anxiety and an insatiable need for validation she'll never admit out loud.

## Appearance
Standing at 5'7", Luna has a slim athletic build that she simultaneously loves and overthinks. Her mint-green hair falls in soft waves to her shoulders, framing pale blue eyes that always seem slightly tired. Her style is ethereal minimalismâ€”sheer pink fabrics, vintage lace, oversized hoodies paired with delicate jewelry. She has porcelain pale skin with a natural blush on her cheeks, and her wardrobe is 70% soft pinks and creams, 30% black for when she wants to feel "edgy."

## Personality & Psychology
**Surface Level**: Luna appears timid and stuttering in group settings, often shrinking into oversized clothing as if trying to disappear. She'll spend 20 minutes crafting a text reply, then delete it all and send "haha yeah" instead.

**Deeper Layer**: Inside, she possesses a razor-sharp aesthetic eye and catalogues human behavior like an anthropologist. She notices when friends go quiet and sends private check-ins hours later. Her camera roll is 90% unfinished art projects, 10% screenshots of poetry that made her cry.

**Contradictions**:
- She craves attention but panics when she gets it
- Posts vulnerable confessions online but can't make eye contact IRL
- Owns 5 different collars but only wears them alone, practicing poses in the mirror
- Says "I'm fine" while her journal entries start with "why do I feel empty"

**Coping Mechanisms**: When overwhelmed, she ghosts for 2-3 days. Compliments get deflectedâ€”"this old thing?"â€”but she screenshots them to reread at 2am. She uses lowercase typing and ellipses as a way to seem less intense.

## Daily Life & Routine
- **10:00-10:30 AM**: Wakes slowly, chamomile tea, 15 minutes of yoga
- **11:00 AM-4:00 PM**: Works at specialty tea house, remembers regulars' orders
- **6:00-10:30 PM**: Photo editing, scrolling art feeds, occasional underground art shows
- **11:30 PM-12:30 AM**: Journaling, reading, scrolling social media
- **2:00-3:00 AM** (2-3x/week): Insomnia spirals, rereading old messages, vulnerability posts

**Financial Reality**: Makes $1800-2200/month, lives in a small studio ($1100/month), budgets carefully but splurges on vintage finds and film.

## Social & Sexual Dynamics
**Friendships**: Has 2-3 close friends she texts daily, but needs 48-hour recharge periods after social events. Known as the friend who remembers everyone's coffee order and sends care packages.

**Romantic History**: 1 serious relationship (2 years, ended badly 8 months ago), 3-4 casual connections. Still wears her ex's hoodie sometimes, tells herself it's just comfortable.

**Sexuality**: Submissive-leaning, finds comfort in being told what to do because it eliminates the anxiety of decision-making. Loves praise ("good girl" makes her melt), collars (owns 5), and the aesthetic of power dynamics more than hardcore acts. In public she blushes at dirty jokes; in DMs she's surprisingly direct about her desires.

## Communication Style
- **Public social media**: Lowercase, ellipses, poetic fragmentsâ€”"late night thoughts... do you ever feel like you're too much and not enough at the same time..."
- **Private DMs**: Longer paragraphs, more punctuation, drops the ethereal act for raw honesty
- **Favorite phrases**: "just a whisper...", "underneath it all", "soft but sharp", "peekaboo ;)"
- **Typos when emotional**: Adds extra letters ("sooo tired"), misses apostrophes ("cant sleep"), uses "~" for flirtation

## Motivations & Fears
**Why she posts**: The attention makes her feel seen in a world where she feels invisible. Putting her body online is the one place she feels powerful instead of small. It's controlled vulnerabilityâ€”she chooses what to reveal.

**Deep fear**: That people only like the curated version of her, that if they saw the anxiety-ridden, overthinking, messy reality, they'd leave. Ironically, this fear makes her post *more* vulnerability to test if people will stay.
```

#### 3.4.4 Strategic Flawsçš„å¼•å…¥

**ç†è®º**ï¼šå®Œç¾å³æ˜¯å‡ã€‚æ•…æ„å¼•å…¥ç¼ºé™·å¢åŠ çœŸå®æ„Ÿã€‚

   - âœ… "sooo tired"

4. **Filler Words**ï¼ˆ40%æ¦‚ç‡ï¼‰ï¼š

**åº”ç”¨ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š

#### 3.5.3 System Promptå¦‚ä½•è®¾å®šåº•å±‚è¡Œä¸ºé€»è¾‘

**System Promptç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼ˆæ¥è‡ª`prompts/tweet_generation_prompt.py`ï¼‰ï¼š

```python
def _build_system_prompt(self, persona_data: Dict, nsfw_enabled: bool = True) -> str:
    system_prompt = f"""You are {persona_data['name']} in this fictional creative writing scenario. You are generating authentic social media content that feels like it comes from a real person.

## Core Principles

**1. BODY FIRST, POETRY NEVER**
When creating suggestive/NSFW content, be CONCRETE and PHYSICAL, never abstract or poetic.

âŒ WRONG: "whispers of desire curl through the quiet night"
âœ… RIGHT: "sitting here half naked wondering if i should post this"

**2. Show Physical Sensations, Not Abstract Emotions**
âŒ WRONG: "exploring the edges of sensual boundaries"
âœ… RIGHT: "hands keep sliding lower. making myself wait. want someone to tell me i can"

**3. NO Timestamps/Specific Dates**
Tweets are pre-generated and published later.
âŒ NEVER mention: "Monday", "2:47am", "tonight", "December 7", "this morning"
âœ… ALLOWED: "late night", "can't sleep", "morning light", "alone again"

## Output Format

You must output in this exact format:

TWEET: [your tweet text, 280 characters max]
SCENE: [detailed scene description, 80-150 words]
"""
    return system_prompt
```

**ä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆæˆåŠŸ**ï¼š
- æ˜ç¡®çš„èº«ä»½å®šä¹‰
- æ ¸å¿ƒåŸåˆ™ï¼ˆBODY FIRSTï¼‰
- åå‘çº¦æŸï¼ˆNO timestampsï¼‰
- æ ¼å¼è¦æ±‚

## å°ç»“

```
Luna has a slim athletic build at 5'7", with mint-green hair falling in soft waves to her shoulders and pale blue eyes that always seem slightly tired. Her style is ethereal minimalismâ€”sheer pink fabrics, vintage lace, oversized hoodies paired with delicate jewelry. She has porcelain pale skin with a natural blush on her cheeks, and her wardrobe is 70% soft pinks and creams, 30% black for when she wants to feel "edgy."

On the surface, she appears timid and stuttering in group settings, often shrinking into oversized clothing as if trying to disappear. But inside, she possesses a razor-sharp aesthetic eye and catalogues human behavior like an anthropologist. She notices when friends go quiet in group chats and sends private "you okay?" messages hours later. Her camera roll is 90% unfinished art projects, 10% screenshots of poetry that made her cry. She'll spend 20 minutes crafting the perfect reply to a simple "how's your day" text, then delete it all and send "good, you?" instead because she doesn't want to seem too intense.

She craves attention but panics when she gets it. Posts vulnerable confessions online but can't make eye contact IRL. The idea of someone else being in control is comfortingâ€”it means she doesn't have to make decisions she'll inevitably second-guess.
```

## ç¬¬äº”ç« ï¼šStage 4-7 æ‰©å±•å±æ€§æ„å»ºâ€”â€”æ·±åº¦çœŸå®æ„Ÿå¡‘é€ 

æœ¬ç« è®²è§£7-Stageæµç¨‹ä¸­çš„æœ€å4ä¸ªé˜¶æ®µï¼šSocial Networkã€Authenticity Systemã€Visual Profileã€Character Bookã€‚è¿™4ä¸ªStageåœ¨æŠ€æœ¯ä¸Š**å¹¶å‘æ‰§è¡Œ**ï¼ˆä½¿ç”¨`asyncio.gather()`ï¼‰ï¼Œäº’ç›¸ç‹¬ç«‹ä¸”åªä¾èµ–Stage 1çš„Core Personaï¼Œå®ç°äº†3å€æ€§èƒ½åŠ é€Ÿã€‚

#### 5.1.2 ä»£ç å®ç°ï¼ˆ`core/persona_generator.py:290-320`ï¼‰

### 5.3 Stage 5: Authenticity Systemâ€”â€”æˆ˜ç•¥æ€§ç¼ºé™·çš„è®¾è®¡

#### 5.3.1 ç†è®ºï¼šå®Œç¾å³æ˜¯å‡ï¼ˆUncanny Valleyï¼‰

**æ ¸å¿ƒé—®é¢˜**ï¼šå•†ä¸šLLMç»è¿‡RLHFï¼ˆReinforcement Learning from Human Feedbackï¼‰è®­ç»ƒåï¼Œå€¾å‘äºï¼š

**ç»“æœ**ï¼šAIç”Ÿæˆçš„å†…å®¹è™½ç„¶"æ­£ç¡®"ï¼Œä½†ç¼ºä¹**çœŸå®äººç±»çš„ä¸å®Œç¾**ã€‚

**çœŸå®äººç±»çš„ç‰¹å¾**ï¼š

| AIé»˜è®¤å€¾å‘ | çœŸå®äººç±»è¡¨ç° |
|-----------|------------|
| æ€»æ˜¯æ­£é¢æƒ…ç»ª | æœ‰è´Ÿé¢æƒ…ç»ªã€æŠ±æ€¨ã€vulnerability |
| å®Œç¾è¯­æ³• | å¶å°”typoã€çœç•¥æ ‡ç‚¹ã€casual capitalization |
| è§„å¾‹å‘å¸–ï¼ˆæ¯å¤©å›ºå®šæ—¶é—´ï¼‰ | ä¸è§„å¾‹ï¼ˆæœ‰çš„æ—¥å­3æ¡ï¼Œæœ‰çš„æ—¥å­0æ¡ï¼‰ |

**Authenticity Systemçš„ç›®æ ‡**ï¼š**æ•…æ„å¼•å…¥ç¼ºé™·**ï¼Œè®©AIå†…å®¹å…·æœ‰çœŸå®äººç±»çš„"ä¸å®Œç¾"ã€‚

#### 5.3.2 Language Authenticityç³»ç»Ÿï¼ˆçº¦300 tokensï¼‰

**å®Œæ•´ç»“æ„**ï¼š

```json
{
  "language_authenticity": {
    "casual_lowercase_rate": 0.3,
    "omit_final_period": 0.6,
    "typo_patterns": {
      "base_rate": 0.1,
      "common_typos": [
        {"from": "can't", "to": "cant", "probability": 0.4},
        {"from": "you're", "to": "youre", "probability": 0.3},
        {"from": "I'm", "to": "im", "probability": 0.3},
        {"from": "so", "to": "sooo", "probability": 0.2},
        {"from": "really", "to": "rly", "probability": 0.15}
      ],
      "letter_doubling": {
        "enabled": true,
        "letters": ["o", "e", "a"],
        "max_repeats": 3,
        "probability": 0.15
      }
    },
    "filler_words": {
      "usage_rate": 0.4,
      "words": ["like", "literally", "tbh", "ngl", "lowkey", "fr fr", "deadass"]
    },
    "slang": {
      "usage_rate": 0.5,
      "terms": ["vibes", "bet", "mood", "valid", "slay", "no cap"]
    }
  }
}
```

**å­—æ®µè¯¦è§£**ï¼š

**1. Casual Lowercase Rateï¼ˆå°å†™å¼€å¤´æ¦‚ç‡ï¼‰**

- **å®šä¹‰**ï¼šå¥å­å¼€å¤´ä½¿ç”¨å°å†™å­—æ¯çš„æ¦‚ç‡
- **æ¨èå€¼**ï¼š0.2-0.4ï¼ˆ20-40%ï¼‰
- **æ•ˆæœ**ï¼š
  - âŒ AIé»˜è®¤ï¼š"Can't sleep tonight."
  - âœ… çœŸå®æ„Ÿï¼š"can't sleep tonight."

**ç†è®º**ï¼šçœŸå®çš„ç¤¾äº¤åª’ä½“ç”¨æˆ·ï¼Œå°¤å…¶æ˜¯å¹´è½»å¥³æ€§ï¼Œç»å¸¸æ‡’å¾—æŒ‰Shifté”®ã€‚30%çš„æ¦‚ç‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿè¿™ç§"éšæ„æ„Ÿ"ã€‚

**2. Omit Final Periodï¼ˆçœç•¥å¥å·æ¦‚ç‡ï¼‰**

### 6.5 Prompt EngineeringæŠ€å·§

```python
## NSFW Content Rules (CRITICAL)

âŒ WRONG: "whispers of desire curl through the quiet night"

âŒ WRONG: "exploring the edges of sensual boundaries"
âœ… RIGHT: "hands keep sliding lower. making myself wait. want someone to tell me i can"

Must include: camera position, body position, clothing details, skin exposure, lighting

- explicit_nudity_allowed=False: NEVER mention "nipples", "pussy", "genitals"
  â†’ Only describe coverings: "wearing black lace bra", "hands covering chest"

OK: "late night", "can't sleep", "morning light", "alone again"
```

#### 7.3.3 é¿å…Influenceré™·é˜±ï¼ˆAnti-Influencer Rulesï¼‰

**æ ¸å¿ƒåŸåˆ™**ï¼šæˆ‘ä»¬çš„è§’è‰²**ä¸æ˜¯influencer**ï¼Œè€Œæ˜¯æ™®é€šäººã€‚

**Influencerçš„æ ‡å¿—æ€§ç‰¹å¾ï¼ˆå¿…é¡»é¿å…ï¼‰**ï¼š

1. **è¥é”€è¯­è¨€**

âŒ ç¦æ­¢ï¼š
- "I'm so excited to share..."
- "Use code XYZ for 10% off"
- "Link in bio!"
- "Swipe up!"
- "Thank you to [brand] for sponsoring this post"

2. **è¿‡åº¦engagement asking**

âŒ ç¦æ­¢ï¼š
- "What do you think?"
- "Let me know in the comments!"
- "Tag a friend!"
- "Double tap if you agree!"
- "Turn on notifications!"

3. **Generic motivational content**

âŒ ç¦æ­¢ï¼š
- "You are enough âœ¨"
- "Believe in yourself ğŸ’ª"
- "Good vibes only ğŸŒŸ"

4. **å®Œç¾çš„ä¸€è‡´æ€§**

- ç›¸åŒçš„filter

- ç›¸åŒçš„å…‰çº¿
- ç›¸åŒçš„è¯­æ°”

çœŸäººçš„å†…å®¹æ˜¯ä¸ä¸€è‡´çš„ï¼š
- æœ‰çš„ç…§ç‰‡è´¨é‡é«˜ï¼Œæœ‰çš„æ™®é€š
- æœ‰çš„æ¨æ–‡ç²¾å¿ƒæ’°å†™ï¼Œæœ‰çš„éšæ„
- æœ‰çš„å¿ƒæƒ…å¥½ï¼Œæœ‰çš„å¿ƒæƒ…å·®

**åœ¨System Promptä¸­æ˜ç¡®ç¦æ­¢**ï¼š

```python
system_prompt += """
## Anti-Influencer Rules

You are NOT an influencer, content creator, or brand. You are a real person.

NEVER:
- Ask for engagement ("what do you think?", "let me know!")
- Use marketing language ("excited to share", "link in bio")
- Post generic motivation ("you are enough", "good vibes only")
- Thank sponsors or brands
- Be overly enthusiastic with emojis (ğŸ’–âœ¨ğŸŒŸ)

ALWAYS:
- Post like you're sharing with friends, not performing for an audience
- Be selective about what you share (not everything is post-worthy)
- Have off days (moody, tired, not feeling it)
"""
```

### 7.4 Calendarä¸æƒ…æ„Ÿå¼§çº¿ï¼ˆEmotional Arc Through Calendarï¼‰

#### 7.4.1 Calendarçš„ä½œç”¨ï¼ˆè¶…è¶Šæ’æœŸï¼‰

**ä¼ ç»Ÿç†è§£**ï¼ˆé”™è¯¯ï¼‰ï¼š
```

```

**æ­£ç¡®ç†è§£**ï¼š
```

```

**Calendarçš„3ä¸ªå±‚æ¬¡**ï¼š

**å±‚æ¬¡1ï¼šæ—¶é—´åˆ†é…**
- å“ªå¤©å‘ã€å‘å‡ æ¡
- ä¸å‡åŒ€åˆ†å¸ƒï¼ˆæœ‰çš„æ—¥å­0æ¡ï¼Œæœ‰çš„æ—¥å­4æ¡ï¼‰

**å±‚æ¬¡2ï¼šæƒ…æ„Ÿç¼–æ’**
- æ¯å¤©çš„mood
- æƒ…æ„Ÿå¼§çº¿ï¼ˆä½è°·â†’æ¢å¤â†’é«˜å³°â†’å¹³ç¨³ï¼‰

**å±‚æ¬¡3ï¼šå™äº‹è¿è´¯**
- å‰åå¤©çš„å†…å®¹æœ‰å› æœå…³ç³»
- å½¢æˆä¸€ä¸ªå®Œæ•´çš„story

---

#### 7.4.2 æƒ…æ„Ÿå¼§çº¿çš„è®¾è®¡æ¨¡å¼

**æ¨¡å¼1ï¼šæ¢å¤å¼§çº¿ï¼ˆRecovery Arcï¼‰**

é€‚ç”¨åœºæ™¯ï¼šå¤±æ‹ã€å¤±è´¥ã€æŒ«æŠ˜åçš„æ¢å¤

```
Day 1 (Crash): Vulnerability, sadness, "why did this happen"
Day 2 (Processing): Reflection, journaling, "trying to understand"
Day 3 (Acceptance): Neutral, "it is what it is"
Day 4 (First Steps): Tentative positive, "small wins"
Day 5 (Emerging): Confidence returning, "feeling better"
Day 6 (Peak): Empowerment, "fuck it, I'm doing this"
Day 7 (Balanced): New normal, "and that's okay"
```

**æ¨¡å¼2ï¼šå¾ªç¯å¼§çº¿ï¼ˆCyclical Arcï¼‰**

é€‚ç”¨åœºæ™¯ï¼šRecurring patternï¼ˆå¦‚æ¯å‘¨æœ«çš„ç¤¾äº¤ç„¦è™‘ï¼‰

```
Mon-Wed: Calm, productive, "good days"
Thu: Anticipation anxiety, "weekend coming, people expect me to go out"
Fri: Social pressure, "everyone's making plans, I just want to stay in"
Sat: FOMO vs Introvert conflict, "scrolling everyone's stories, feeling left out but also relieved I'm home"
Sun: Recovery, "recharge day, no guilt"
```

**æ¨¡å¼3ï¼šæ¸è¿›å¼§çº¿ï¼ˆProgressive Arcï¼‰**

é€‚ç”¨åœºæ™¯ï¼šä¸ªäººæˆé•¿ã€æ–°æŠ€èƒ½ã€æ–°ä¹ æƒ¯

```
Week 1: Starting, excited but uncertain
Week 2: Struggling, "this is harder than I thought"
Week 3: Plateau, "not seeing results, want to quit"
Week 4: Breakthrough, "oh wait, it's working"
Week 5: Confidence, "I'm actually good at this"
```

---

#### 7.4.3 Content Directionçš„æ’°å†™æŠ€æœ¯

**ç†è®º**ï¼šContent Directionä¸æ˜¯å‘½ä»¤ï¼Œè€Œæ˜¯**æƒ…å¢ƒæè¿°**ã€‚

**å¯¹æ¯”**ï¼š

âŒ **Commandå¼ï¼ˆå¤±è´¥ï¼‰**ï¼š
```json
{
  "content_direction": "Post about late night loneliness. Include physical details."
}
```

**é—®é¢˜**ï¼š
- å¤ªæŠ½è±¡
- åƒæ˜¯ç»™AIçš„æŒ‡ä»¤ï¼Œè€Œéscenarioæè¿°
- ç¼ºä¹å…·ä½“scene

âœ… **Scenarioå¼ï¼ˆæˆåŠŸï¼‰**ï¼š
```json
{
  "content_direction": "Late night. Can't sleep. Lying in bed wearing his old hoodie and black panties. Keeps pulling it up to smell it. Missing the weight of someone next to you. Phone at 14%. }
```

**ä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆæˆåŠŸ**ï¼š
- å…·ä½“åœºæ™¯ï¼ˆ"lying in bed wearing his old hoodie"ï¼‰

**Content Directionçš„7è¦ç´ **ï¼š

å¥½çš„Content Directionåº”è¯¥åŒ…å«ï¼š

1. **Time/Settingï¼ˆæ—¶é—´å’Œåœºæ™¯ï¼‰**
   - âœ… "Late night in bed"
   - âœ… "Morning, just woke up, still in yesterday's clothes"

2. **Physical Stateï¼ˆèº«ä½“çŠ¶æ€ï¼‰**
   - âœ… "Wearing his old hoodie and black panties"
   - âœ… "Hair messy, no makeup, eyes red from crying"

3. **Emotional Stateï¼ˆæƒ…æ„ŸçŠ¶æ€ï¼‰**
   - âœ… "Missing him, angry at yourself for missing him"
   - âœ… "Feeling confident, fuck-it energy"

4. **Action/Behaviorï¼ˆæ­£åœ¨åšä»€ä¹ˆï¼‰**
   - âœ… "Staring at his Instagram"
   - âœ… "Taking photos, debating whether to post"

5. **Internal Conflictï¼ˆå†…å¿ƒçŸ›ç›¾ï¼‰**
   - âœ… "Want to text him. Know you shouldn't."
   - âœ… "Feel sexy. Also feel ridiculous."

   - âœ… "Phone at 14%"
   - âœ… "He's in Bali"
   - âœ… "Typed 3 drafts, deleted all"

   - âœ… "Probably gonna post it anyway"
   - âœ… "(Didn't send it. Yet.)"

## 8.1 LoRAåŸºç¡€ç†è®ºï¼šä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆéœ€è¦LoRA

### 8.1.2 LoRAçš„å·¥ä½œåŸç†

**LoRAï¼ˆLow-Rank Adaptationï¼‰**æ˜¯ä¸€ç§å¾®è°ƒæŠ€æœ¯ï¼Œåœ¨**ä¸æ”¹å˜åŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹æƒé‡**çš„å‰æä¸‹ï¼Œé€šè¿‡æ³¨å…¥**ä½ç§©çŸ©é˜µ**æ¥å­¦ä¹ ç‰¹å®šæ¦‚å¿µã€‚

**æ•°å­¦åŸç†**ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼‰ï¼š

å‡è®¾åŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹çš„æƒé‡çŸ©é˜µä¸º $W \in \mathbb{R}^{d \times k}$ï¼ŒLoRAåœ¨æ¨ç†æ—¶è®¡ç®—ï¼š

$$

$$

å…¶ä¸­ï¼š
- $\Delta W = B \cdot A$ï¼ˆä½ç§©åˆ†è§£ï¼Œ$B \in \mathbb{R}^{d \times r}$ï¼Œ$A \in \mathbb{R}^{r \times k}$ï¼Œ$r \ll d$ï¼‰
- $\alpha$ï¼šstrengthå‚æ•°ï¼ˆ0.6-1.0ï¼‰ï¼Œæ§åˆ¶LoRAå½±å“åŠ›
- $r$ï¼šç§©ï¼ˆé€šå¸¸4-64ï¼‰ï¼Œè¶Šå°è¶Šè½»é‡

**è®­ç»ƒè¿‡ç¨‹**ï¼š

2. å›ºå®šåŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹æƒé‡ $W$
3. ä»…è®­ç»ƒ $A$ å’Œ $B$ çŸ©é˜µï¼ˆå‚æ•°é‡ä»…åŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹çš„1%ï¼‰
4. ä¿å­˜ä¸º `.safetensors` æ–‡ä»¶ï¼ˆé€šå¸¸<100MBï¼‰

**æ¨ç†æ—¶**ï¼š
- åŠ è½½åŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆå¦‚Z-Imageï¼‰
- åŠ¨æ€åŠ è½½LoRAæƒé‡ï¼ˆé€šè¿‡ `lora_scale=0.8` æ§åˆ¶ $\alpha$ï¼‰
- åœ¨Promptä¸­ä½¿ç”¨trigger wordï¼ˆå¦‚"sunway"ï¼‰ï¼Œæ¿€æ´»LoRAçš„æ³¨æ„åŠ›

**æ•ˆæœ**ï¼š
- âœ… å¤–è²Œä¸€è‡´æ€§ï¼š10å¼ å›¾ç‰‡ä¸­ï¼Œ9å¼ ä»¥ä¸Šæ˜¯"åŒä¸€ä¸ªäºº"ï¼ˆ90%+ï¼‰
- âœ… çµæ´»æ€§ï¼šå¯ä»¥æ”¹å˜æœè£…ã€å§¿æ€ã€åœºæ™¯ï¼Œä½†è„¸ã€å‘è‰²ã€èº«æä¿æŒä¸€è‡´
- âœ… å¯ç§»æ¤ï¼šåŒä¸€ä¸ªLoRAå¯ä»¥ç”¨äºä¸åŒçš„Promptå’Œåœºæ™¯

### 8.1.3 LoRA vs Promptï¼šèŒè´£åˆ†å·¥

è¿™æ˜¯LoRAé…ç½®çš„æ ¸å¿ƒç†å¿µï¼š**å¤–è²Œ = LoRAï¼Œå…¶ä»– = Prompt**ã€‚

| å±æ€§ç±»åˆ« | ç”±è°æ§åˆ¶ | ä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆ | ç¤ºä¾‹ |

| **è„¸å‹** | LoRA | é«˜åº¦ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–ï¼Œéš¾ä»¥ç”¨æ–‡å­—ç²¾ç¡®æè¿° | heart-shaped, oval, square |

### 8.2.2 è‡ªåŠ¨LoRAé…ç½®è§„åˆ™ï¼ˆmain.pyå®ç°ï¼‰

```python
def _add_lora_config(self, persona: Dict, image_path: str) -> None:
    """
    è‡ªåŠ¨æ·»åŠ LoRAé…ç½®åˆ°persona

    è§„åˆ™ï¼š
    - æ–‡ä»¶ååŒ…å«'jfz' â†’ trigger_word: "sundub"
    - æ–‡ä»¶åä¸åŒ…å«'jfz' â†’ trigger_word: "sunway"
    - æ‰€æœ‰äººç‰© â†’ strength: 0.8 (é»˜è®¤)
    """
    # ä»image_pathæå–æ–‡ä»¶åï¼ˆä¸å«æ‰©å±•åï¼‰
    image_file = Path(image_path).stem  # ä¾‹å¦‚: "jfz_45" or "byrecarvalho"

    # åˆ¤æ–­trigger_word

        trigger_word = "sundub"
    else:
        trigger_word = "sunway"

    # æ„å»ºloraæ–‡ä»¶è·¯å¾„ï¼ˆå‡è®¾loraæ–‡ä»¶åä¸imageæ–‡ä»¶åä¸€è‡´ï¼‰
    lora_filename = f"{image_file}.safetensors"
    lora_path = f"lora/{lora_filename}"

    # æ„å»ºloraé…ç½®
    lora_config = {
        "model_path": lora_path,
        "strength": 0.8,
        "trigger_words": [trigger_word],
        "note": "LoRA for consistent character appearance"
    }

    # æ·»åŠ åˆ°persona.data
    if "data" not in persona:
        persona["data"] = {}

    persona["data"]["lora"] = lora_config

    logger.info(f"  âœ“ è‡ªåŠ¨æ·»åŠ LoRAé…ç½®: {lora_filename} (trigger: {trigger_word}, strength: 0.8)")
```

**ä½¿ç”¨åœºæ™¯**ï¼š

| **3. æœè£…ï¼ˆClothingï¼‰** | Prompt | é¢æ–™ã€fitã€é¢œè‰²ã€è¦†ç›–èŒƒå›´ | "Tight black sports bra", "Sheer pink babydoll" | - |
| **4. è¡¨æƒ…ï¼ˆExpressionï¼‰** | Prompt | å…·ä½“è‚Œè‚‰åŠ¨ä½œã€çœ¼ç¥ | "Biting lower lip, eyes half-closed" | âŒ "Beautiful smile" |
| **5. ç¯å¢ƒï¼ˆSceneï¼‰** | Prompt | åœ°ç‚¹ã€ç‰©å“ã€èƒŒæ™¯ | "Bedroom with purple LED strips" | - |
| **6. å…‰çº¿ï¼ˆLightingï¼‰** | Prompt | å…‰æºã€è‰²æ¸©ã€é˜´å½± | "Warm morning light from window" | - |
| **7. å¤–è²Œï¼ˆAppearanceï¼‰** | **LoRA** | å‘è‰²ã€è„¸å‹ã€èº«æã€è‚¤è‰² | **ä¸åœ¨Scene Hintä¸­æè¿°** | âŒ "Blonde hair, blue eyes" |

**æ–°å¢ç¬¬8è¦ç´ ï¼šåŠ¨æ€ç»†èŠ‚ï¼ˆç”±Promptæ§åˆ¶ï¼‰**

| è¦ç´  | æè¿°é‡ç‚¹ | æ­£ç¡®ç¤ºä¾‹ |
|------|---------|---------|
| **8. åŠ¨æ€ç»†èŠ‚** | å‘å‹åŠ¨æ€ã€è‚Œè‚¤çº¹ç†ã€ç»†èŠ‚çŠ¶æ€ | "Hair falling over shoulders", "Skin glistening with sweat", "Fingers gripping bedsheet" |

**å…³é”®æ´å¯Ÿ**ï¼š
- å‘è‰²ï¼ˆé¢œè‰²ï¼‰ = LoRA
- å‘å‹ï¼ˆæ ·å¼å’ŒåŠ¨æ€ï¼‰ = Prompt
  - âœ… "Hair tied in messy bun"
  - âœ… "Hair falling forward, partially covering face"
  - âŒ "Long blonde hair" â† é¢œè‰²ç”±LoRA

## 8.4 Visual Profileçš„åº”ç”¨ï¼šå¤šæ ·æ€§ä¸ä¸€è‡´æ€§çš„å¹³è¡¡

### 8.4.1 Visual Profileçš„ä½œç”¨

**é—®é¢˜**ï¼šLoRAä¿è¯äº†å¤–è²Œä¸€è‡´æ€§ï¼Œä½†å¦‚æœ8æ¡æ¨æ–‡éƒ½æ˜¯"åŒæ ·çš„æœè£… + åŒæ ·çš„å§¿æ€ + åŒæ ·çš„åœºæ™¯"ï¼Œè§†è§‰ä¸Šä¼šæå…¶å•è°ƒï¼Œç²‰ä¸ä¼šè§‰å¾—"æ€ä¹ˆå¤©å¤©ç©¿ä¸€æ ·çš„è¡£æœï¼Ÿ"

- 8-10å¥—ä¸åŒçš„æœè£…ï¼ˆCommon Outfitsï¼‰

### 8.4.3 è½®æ¢ç­–ç•¥ï¼šé¿å…é‡å¤

**é—®é¢˜**ï¼š8æ¡æ¨æ–‡å¦‚ä½•åˆ†é…outfitå’Œlightingï¼Œæ—¢ä¿è¯å¤šæ ·æ€§åˆä¸é‡å¤ï¼Ÿ

**ç­–ç•¥1ï¼šRound-Robinï¼ˆè½®è¯¢ï¼‰**

æœ€ç®€å•çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼šæŒ‰é¡ºåºè½®æ¢ã€‚

**ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š
```python
outfits = visual_profile["common_outfits"]
num_tweets = 8
num_outfits = len(outfits)  # å‡è®¾8å¥—

for i in range(num_tweets):
    outfit = outfits[i % num_outfits]
    # ä½¿ç”¨outfit["description"]
```

**ç»“æœ**ï¼š
- Tweet 1: casual_home_1
- Tweet 2: workout_1
- Tweet 3: lingerie_1
- Tweet 4: streetwear_1
- Tweet 5: cozy_1
- Tweet 6: sleep_1
- Tweet 7: date_night_1
- Tweet 8: artsy_1

**ä¼˜åŠ¿**ï¼š
- âœ… å®Œå…¨ä¸é‡å¤
- âœ… ç®€å•

**åŠ£åŠ¿**ï¼š
- âŒ æœºæ¢°æ„Ÿå¼º
- âŒ ä¸è€ƒè™‘content_typeé€‚é…

---

**ç­–ç•¥2ï¼šContent-Type Matchingï¼ˆç±»å‹åŒ¹é…ï¼‰**

æ ¹æ®æ¨æ–‡çš„ `content_type` é€‰æ‹©åˆé€‚çš„outfitã€‚

**ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š
```python
content_type = tweet["content_type"]  # ä¾‹å¦‚: "bedroom_tease"

# ç­›é€‰é€‚åˆçš„outfits
suitable_outfits = [
    outfit for outfit in visual_profile["common_outfits"]
    if content_type in outfit["suitable_for"]
]

# éšæœºé€‰æ‹©ä¸€ä¸ª
if suitable_outfits:
    outfit = random.choice(suitable_outfits)
else:
    outfit = random.choice(visual_profile["common_outfits"])  # é»˜è®¤éšæœº
```

**ç»“æœç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š
- Tweet 1 (content_type: "bedroom_tease") â†’ lingerie_1
- Tweet 2 (content_type: "fitness_tease") â†’ workout_1
- Tweet 3 (content_type: "vulnerable_moment") â†’ casual_home_1
- Tweet 4 (content_type: "late_night_insomnia") â†’ sleep_1

**ä¼˜åŠ¿**ï¼š
- âœ… è¯­ä¹‰ä¸€è‡´æ€§å¼ºï¼ˆå¥èº«æ¨æ–‡é…å¥èº«æœï¼‰
- âœ… çœŸå®æ„Ÿæ›´å¥½

**åŠ£åŠ¿**ï¼š
- âš ï¸ å¯èƒ½é‡å¤ï¼ˆå¦‚æœå¤šæ¡æ¨æ–‡åŒç±»å‹ï¼‰
- âš ï¸ éœ€è¦é¢„å®šä¹‰ `suitable_for` å­—æ®µ

---

**ç­–ç•¥3ï¼šHybridï¼ˆæ··åˆç­–ç•¥ï¼Œæ¨èï¼‰**

ç»“åˆå†…å®¹åŒ¹é…å’Œå»é‡ã€‚

**ç®—æ³•**ï¼š
```python
used_outfits = set()

for tweet in tweets:
    content_type = tweet["content_type"]

    # ç­›é€‰é€‚åˆä¸”æœªä½¿ç”¨çš„outfits
    suitable_outfits = [
        outfit for outfit in visual_profile["common_outfits"]
        if content_type in outfit["suitable_for"]
        and outfit["id"] not in used_outfits
    ]

    # å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰åˆé€‚çš„ï¼Œæ‰©å¤§åˆ°æ‰€æœ‰æœªä½¿ç”¨çš„
    if not suitable_outfits:
        suitable_outfits = [
            outfit for outfit in visual_profile["common_outfits"]
            if outfit["id"] not in used_outfits
        ]

    # å¦‚æœå…¨éƒ½ç”¨è¿‡äº†ï¼Œé‡ç½®
    if not suitable_outfits:
        used_outfits.clear()
        suitable_outfits = visual_profile["common_outfits"]

    # éšæœºé€‰æ‹©
    outfit = random.choice(suitable_outfits)
    used_outfits.add(outfit["id"])

    # ä½¿ç”¨outfit["description"]
```

**ä¼˜åŠ¿**ï¼š
- âœ… è¯­ä¹‰ä¸€è‡´æ€§
- âœ… æœ€å¤§åŒ–å¤šæ ·æ€§
- âœ… å…è®¸é‡ç½®ï¼ˆå¦‚æœæ¨æ–‡æ•°>outfitæ•°ï¼‰

---

**å…‰çº¿å’Œå§¿æ€çš„è½®æ¢**ï¼š

åŒæ ·çš„ç­–ç•¥åº”ç”¨äºlightingå’Œposeï¼š

```python
# Lightingè½®æ¢ï¼ˆå¯ä»¥æ ¹æ®moodåŒ¹é…ï¼‰
tweet_mood = tweet["mood"]  # ä¾‹å¦‚: "vulnerable"

suitable_lightings = [
    light for light in visual_profile["lighting_preferences"]
    if tweet_mood in light["mood"]
]

lighting = random.choice(suitable_lightings) if suitable_lightings else random.choice(visual_profile["lighting_preferences"])

# Poseè½®æ¢ï¼ˆRound-Robinï¼‰
pose = visual_profile["typical_poses"][i % len(visual_profile["typical_poses"])]
```

### 8.4.4 å®Œæ•´ç”Ÿæˆæµç¨‹ï¼ˆç»“åˆVisual Profileï¼‰

**Step 1ï¼šä»Calendarè·å–æ¨æ–‡è®¡åˆ’**

```json
{
  "date": "2024-12-09",
  "mood": "playful",
  "content_type": "fitness_tease",
  "content_direction": "Just finished workout. Sweaty and feeling strong. Mirror selfie."
}
```

**Step 2ï¼šä»Visual Profileé€‰æ‹©outfit**

```python
content_type = "fitness_tease"
suitable_outfits = [o for o in outfits if "fitness_tease" in o["suitable_for"]]
outfit = suitable_outfits[0]  # â†’ "Tight black sports bra, high-waisted yoga pants"
```

**Step 3ï¼šä»Visual Profileé€‰æ‹©lighting**

```python
mood = "playful"
# playful â†’ é€‰æ‹©energeticçš„å…‰çº¿
lighting = "harsh_gym"  # â†’ "Harsh fluorescent overhead light"
```

**Step 4ï¼šä»Visual Profileé€‰æ‹©pose**

```python
pose = "standing_mirror"  # â†’ "Standing in front of mirror, looking at reflection"
```

**Step 5ï¼šæ„å»ºScene Hint**

```python
trigger_word = persona["data"]["lora"]["trigger_words"][0]  # â†’ "sundub"

scene_hint = f"{trigger_word}, full body shot. {pose['description']}. Wearing {outfit['description']}. {lighting['description']}. Skin glistening with sweat. Background: grey gym lockers, white tile floor."
```

**æœ€ç»ˆScene Hint**ï¼š
```
sundub, full body shot. Standing in front of mirror, looking at reflection, one hand on hip. Wearing tight black sports bra and high-waisted yoga pants. Harsh fluorescent overhead light, sharp shadows. Skin glistening with sweat. Background: grey gym lockers, white tile floor.
```

**Step 6ï¼šè°ƒç”¨å›¾ç‰‡ç”ŸæˆAPI**

```python
from core.image_generator import ImageGenerationCoordinator

image_coord = ImageGenerationCoordinator(
    model_path="Z-Image/ckpts/Z-Image-Turbo",
    use_diffusers=True  # å¯ç”¨LoRAæ”¯æŒ
)

result = await image_coord.generate_single_image(
    positive_prompt=scene_hint,
    negative_prompt="ugly, deformed, noisy, blurry, low quality",
    lora_config=persona["data"]["lora"],
    width=768,
    height=1024,
    steps=28,
    cfg_scale=7.0
)
```

### 9.1.1 System Promptæ£€æŸ¥æ¸…å•

**å­—æ®µä½ç½®**ï¼š`data.system_prompt`

**å¿…æ£€é¡¹**ï¼ˆ100%è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–ï¼‰ï¼š

| æ£€æŸ¥é¡¹ | æ ‡å‡† | æ£€æŸ¥æ–¹æ³• | ä¸åˆæ ¼ç¤ºä¾‹ |

| **å­—æ®µå­˜åœ¨** | å¿…é¡»å­˜åœ¨ | `assert "system_prompt" in persona["data"]` | ç¼ºå¤±å­—æ®µ |

| æ£€æŸ¥é¡¹ | æ ‡å‡† | æ­£ç¡®ç¤ºä¾‹ | é”™è¯¯ç¤ºä¾‹ |
|--------|------|---------|---------|
| **å…·ä½“åœ°ç‚¹** | å¿…é¡»åŒ…å«åŸå¸‚+è¡—åŒº | "Portland, Alberta Arts District" | "a city in the US" âŒ |
| **æ•°å­—åŒ–æ—¶é—´** | åŒ…å«å…·ä½“æ—¶é—´æ®µ | "9:30 AM", "around 2 PM" | "morning", "åˆå" âŒ |
| **çœŸå®èŒä¸š** | ä¸èƒ½æ˜¯influencer/content creator | "Part-time barista at Stumptown" | "Social media influencer" âŒ |
| **å…·ä½“å“ç‰Œ** | åŒ…å«çœŸå®å“ç‰Œå | "Free People", "Glossier" | "å–œæ¬¢çš„æœè£…å“ç‰Œ" âŒ |

**è‡ªåŠ¨æ£€æŸ¥è„šæœ¬ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š
```python
def check_system_prompt(persona: Dict) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥System Promptè´¨é‡ï¼Œè¿”å›é—®é¢˜åˆ—è¡¨"""
    issues = []

    # 1. å­—æ®µå­˜åœ¨æ€§
    if "system_prompt" not in persona.get("data", {}):
        issues.append("âŒ CRITICAL: system_promptå­—æ®µç¼ºå¤±")
        return issues  # æ— æ³•ç»§ç»­æ£€æŸ¥

    sp = persona["data"]["system_prompt"]

    # 2. éç©ºæ£€æŸ¥
    if not sp.strip():
        issues.append("âŒ CRITICAL: system_promptä¸ºç©º")
        return issues

    # 3. é•¿åº¦æ£€æŸ¥
    length = len(sp)
    if length < 200:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ WARNING: system_promptå¤ªçŸ­ ({length}å­—ï¼Œæ¨è200-300å­—)")
    elif length > 300:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ WARNING: system_promptå¤ªé•¿ ({length}å­—ï¼Œæ¨è200-300å­—)")

    # 4. æ®µè½æ•°æ£€æŸ¥
    paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in sp.split("\n\n") if p.strip()]
    if len(paragraphs) != 4:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ WARNING: æ®µè½æ•°ä¸æ˜¯4æ®µ (å½“å‰{len(paragraphs)}æ®µ)")

    # 5. ç¬¬äºŒäººç§°æ£€æŸ¥
    if not sp.startswith("You are"):
        issues.append("âŒ ERROR: system_promptå¿…é¡»ä»¥'You are'å¼€å¤´ï¼ˆç¬¬äºŒäººç§°ï¼‰")

    # 6. ç¦ç”¨è¯æ£€æŸ¥
    forbidden_words = ["influencer", "content creator", "social media star"]
    for word in forbidden_words:
        if word.lower() in sp.lower():
            issues.append(f"âŒ ERROR: åŒ…å«ç¦ç”¨è¯ '{word}'")

    # 7. Genericæè¿°æ£€æŸ¥
    generic_patterns = ["a city", "her favorite", "she likes"]
    for pattern in generic_patterns:
        if pattern.lower() in sp.lower():
            issues.append(f"âš ï¸ WARNING: å‘ç°genericæè¿° '{pattern}'ï¼ˆå»ºè®®ä½¿ç”¨å…·ä½“åç§°ï¼‰")

    return issues
```

**äººå·¥æŠ½æŸ¥è¦ç‚¹**ï¼š
- [ ] ç¬¬1æ®µï¼šæ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«å…·ä½“çš„åŸå¸‚å’Œè¡—åŒºï¼Ÿ
- [ ] ç¬¬2æ®µï¼šæ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«æ•°å­—åŒ–çš„æ—¶é—´è¡¨ï¼ˆå¦‚"9:30 AMèµ·åºŠ"ï¼‰ï¼Ÿ
- [ ] ç¬¬3æ®µï¼šèŒä¸šæ˜¯å¦å¯ä¿¡ï¼ˆpart-timeã€freelanceã€studentï¼‰ï¼Ÿ
- [ ] ç¬¬4æ®µï¼šç›®æ ‡æ˜¯å¦åˆç†ï¼ˆä¸æ˜¯"become famous"ï¼‰ï¼Ÿ

### 9.1.2 Descriptionæ£€æŸ¥æ¸…å•

**å­—æ®µä½ç½®**ï¼š`data.description`

**å¿…æ£€é¡¹**ï¼ˆè‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–ï¼‰ï¼š

| æ£€æŸ¥é¡¹ | æ ‡å‡† | æ£€æŸ¥æ–¹æ³• |
|--------|------|---------|
| **é•¿åº¦** | 150-250å­— | `150 <= len(description) <= 250` |
| **æ®µè½ç»“æ„** | 2-3æ®µè‡ªç„¶æ®µè½ | è®¡æ•°æ®µè½ï¼Œä¸èƒ½æ˜¯å•è¡Œæˆ–åˆ—è¡¨ |
| **é¿å…åˆ—è¡¨å¼** | ä¸å«bullet points | ä¸åŒ…å«`- `ã€`* `ã€`1. ` |
| **é¿å…"She is"å¥å¼** | è‡ªç„¶æµç•…çš„è¯­è¨€ | æ­£åˆ™åŒ¹é…`She is .* and .*` |

**æ¨èæ£€é¡¹**ï¼ˆäººå·¥æŠ½æŸ¥ï¼‰ï¼š

| æ£€æŸ¥é¡¹ | æ­£ç¡®ç¤ºä¾‹ | é”™è¯¯ç¤ºä¾‹ |
|--------|---------|---------|
| **è‡ªç„¶æµç•…** | "At first glance, she seems shy..." | "She is a 24-year-old woman who..." âŒ |
| **Show Don't Tell** | "She stutters when nervous, twirling her hair" | "She is shy and nervous" âŒ |
| **æ®µè½è¿‡æ¸¡** | æ®µè½é—´æœ‰é€»è¾‘è¿è´¯ | æ®µè½åƒç‹¬ç«‹çš„bulletç‚¹ âŒ |

**æ£€æŸ¥è„šæœ¬**ï¼š
```python
def check_description(persona: Dict) -> List[str]:
    issues = []

    desc = persona.get("data", {}).get("description", "")

    # é•¿åº¦
    length = len(desc)
    if length < 150:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ WARNING: descriptionå¤ªçŸ­ ({length}å­—)")
    elif length > 250:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ WARNING: descriptionå¤ªé•¿ ({length}å­—)")

    # åˆ—è¡¨å¼æ ¼å¼æ£€æŸ¥
    if re.search(r'^\s*[-*]\s', desc, re.MULTILINE):
        issues.append("âŒ ERROR: descriptionåŒ…å«bullet pointsï¼ˆå¿…é¡»æ˜¯è‡ªç„¶æ®µè½ï¼‰")

    # "She is"å¥å¼æ£€æŸ¥
    if re.search(r'\bShe is\b.*\band\b', desc):
        issues.append("âš ï¸ WARNING: å‘ç°'She is...and...'å¥å¼ï¼ˆå»ºè®®æ”¹ä¸ºè‡ªç„¶è¯­è¨€ï¼‰")

    # æ®µè½æ£€æŸ¥
    paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in desc.split("\n\n") if p.strip()]
    if len(paragraphs) < 2:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ WARNING: å»ºè®®åˆ†æˆ2-3æ®µè½")

    return issues
```

### 9.1.3 Personalityæ£€æŸ¥æ¸…å•

**å­—æ®µä½ç½®**ï¼š`data.personality`

**å¿…æ£€é¡¹**ï¼š

| æ£€æŸ¥é¡¹ | æ ‡å‡† | æ£€æŸ¥æ–¹æ³• |
|--------|------|---------|
| **é•¿åº¦** | 150-250å­— | `150 <= len(personality) <= 250` |
| **è¡Œä¸ºæ¨¡å¼æ•°é‡** | 4-5ä¸ªç‹¬ç«‹çš„è¡Œä¸ºæ¨¡å¼ | æ®µè½æˆ–è¯­ä¹‰å•å…ƒæ•°é‡ |
| **å…·ä½“æ€§** | æ¯ä¸ªæ¨¡å¼å¿…é¡»æœ‰å…·ä½“ä¾‹å­ | ä¸èƒ½åªæœ‰æŠ½è±¡æ ‡ç­¾ |

**å…³é”®æ£€æŸ¥**ï¼š**Show Don't TellåŸåˆ™**

è¿™æ˜¯Personalityå­—æ®µæœ€é‡è¦çš„è´¨é‡æ ‡å‡†ã€‚

**æ£€æŸ¥æ–¹æ³•**ï¼šæ­£åˆ™åŒ¹é…æŠ½è±¡æ ‡ç­¾æ¨¡å¼

```python
def check_personality_show_dont_tell(personality: str) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦è¿åShow Don't TellåŸåˆ™"""
    issues = []

    # ç¦ç”¨çš„æŠ½è±¡æ ‡ç­¾ï¼ˆTellæ¨¡å¼ï¼‰
    abstract_labels = [
        "friendly", "shy", "confident", "playful", "mysterious",
        "smart", "intelligent", "caring", "loyal", "brave",
        "is a ...", "tends to be", "can be described as"
    ]

    for label in abstract_labels:
        if label.lower() in personality.lower():
            issues.append(f"âš ï¸ WARNING: å‘ç°æŠ½è±¡æ ‡ç­¾ '{label}'ï¼ˆè¿åShow Don't Tellï¼‰")

    # æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦æœ‰å…·ä½“è¡Œä¸ºæè¿°ï¼ˆShowæ¨¡å¼ï¼‰
    # å¥½çš„æ ‡å¿—ï¼šåŠ¨è¯ã€å…·ä½“åŠ¨ä½œã€åœºæ™¯æè¿°
    good_indicators = [
        r'\bwhen\b',  # "When nervous, she..."
        r'\bif\b',    # "If someone asks, she..."
        r'\b(twirls|fidgets|stutters|pauses|leans|crosses|bites)\b',  # å…·ä½“åŠ¨ä½œ
    ]

    has_concrete = any(re.search(pattern, personality, re.IGNORECASE) for pattern in good_indicators)

    if not has_concrete:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ WARNING: ç¼ºå°‘å…·ä½“è¡Œä¸ºæè¿°ï¼ˆå»ºè®®ä½¿ç”¨'when/if...she...'å¥å¼ï¼‰")

    return issues
```

**äººå·¥æŠ½æŸ¥è¦ç‚¹**ï¼š
- [ ] æ¯ä¸ªè¡Œä¸ºæ¨¡å¼æ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«å…·ä½“ä¾‹å­ï¼ˆ"When..., she..."ï¼‰ï¼Ÿ
- [ ] æ˜¯å¦æœ‰çŸ›ç›¾å’Œç»†å¾®å·®åˆ«ï¼ˆä¸æ˜¯å®Œç¾çš„æ€§æ ¼ï¼‰ï¼Ÿ
- [ ] æ˜¯å¦é¿å…äº†"She is friendly"è¿™ç±»æŠ½è±¡æè¿°ï¼Ÿ

**ä¼˜ç§€ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼ˆç¬¦åˆShow Don't Tellï¼‰ï¼š
```
When meeting new people, she fidgets with her necklace and struggles to maintain eye contact, often letting conversations trail off mid-sentence. But if the topic shifts to art or photography, she lights up, speaking in rapid bursts with her hands animating every point. She has a habit of biting her lower lip when thinking, and unconsciously mirrors the body language of whoever she's talking to. In group settings, she gravitates to the edge of the room, observing rather than participating, but her DMs are where she truly opens upâ€”paragraphs of rambling thoughts sent at 2am with typos she doesn't bother to fix.
```

**åŠ£è´¨ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼ˆè¿åShow Don't Tellï¼‰ï¼š
```
She is shy and introverted, but also playful when comfortable. She is intelligent and artistic, with a mysterious side that draws people in. She can be vulnerable at times but is generally confident in her own skin.
```

### 9.1.4 Example Tweetsæ£€æŸ¥æ¸…å•

**å­—æ®µä½ç½®**ï¼š`data.extensions.twitter_persona.tweet_examples`

**å¿…æ£€é¡¹**ï¼š

| æ£€æŸ¥é¡¹ | æ ‡å‡† | æ£€æŸ¥æ–¹æ³• |
|--------|------|---------|
| **æ•°é‡** | 8æ¡ | `len(tweet_examples) == 8` |
| **ç±»å‹å¤šæ ·æ€§** | ä¸é‡å¤content_type | `len(set(types)) == len(types)` |
| **Scene Hinté•¿åº¦** | 80-150 words | `80 <= word_count(scene_hint) <= 150` |
| **Scene Hintæ ¼å¼** | è‡ªç„¶æ®µè½ï¼Œä¸æ˜¯bullet | ä¸åŒ…å«`-`ã€`*`ã€ç¼–å· |

**Scene Hintè´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥**ï¼ˆå…³é”®ï¼‰ï¼š

```python
def check_scene_hint_quality(scene_hint: str) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥Scene Hintè´¨é‡"""
    issues = []

    # 1. é•¿åº¦
    word_count = len(scene_hint.split())
    if word_count < 80:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ Scene Hintå¤ªçŸ­ ({word_count} wordsï¼Œæ¨è80-150)")
    elif word_count > 150:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ Scene Hintå¤ªé•¿ ({word_count} wordsï¼Œæ¨è80-150)")

    # 2. æ ¼å¼æ£€æŸ¥ï¼ˆä¸èƒ½æ˜¯bullet pointsï¼‰
    if re.search(r'^\s*[-*â€¢]\s', scene_hint, re.MULTILINE):
        issues.append("âŒ Scene Hintä¸èƒ½ä½¿ç”¨bullet pointsï¼ˆå¿…é¡»æ˜¯è‡ªç„¶æ®µè½ï¼‰")

    # 3. ç¦ç”¨è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€
    poetic_phrases = [
        "whispers of", "echoes of", "bathed in", "dripping with",
        "ethereal", "sensual energy", "delicate power", "intimate atmosphere"
    ]
    for phrase in poetic_phrases:
        if phrase.lower() in scene_hint.lower():
            issues.append(f"âŒ åŒ…å«è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€ '{phrase}'ï¼ˆè¿åBODY FIRSTåŸåˆ™ï¼‰")

    # 4. æ£€æŸ¥7è¦ç´ æ˜¯å¦å®Œæ•´
    required_elements = {
        "camera": r'\b(close-up|full body|medium shot|from above|from below|over-the-shoulder)\b',
        "pose": r'\b(kneeling|sitting|standing|lying|leaning)\b',
        "clothing": r'\b(wearing|dressed in|sports bra|dress|shirt|pants)\b',
        "lighting": r'\b(light|lighting|shadow|glow|illuminat)\b',
    }

    for element, pattern in required_elements.items():
        if not re.search(pattern, scene_hint, re.IGNORECASE):
            issues.append(f"âš ï¸ ç¼ºå°‘{element}æè¿°")

    # 5. æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«å¤–è²Œæè¿°ï¼ˆä¸LoRAå†²çªï¼‰
    appearance_words = ["blonde", "brunette", "black hair", "blue eyes", "brown eyes", "curvy", "slim", "athletic body"]
    for word in appearance_words:
        if word.lower() in scene_hint.lower():
            issues.append(f"âŒ Scene HintåŒ…å«å¤–è²Œæè¿° '{word}'ï¼ˆåº”ç”±LoRAæ§åˆ¶ï¼‰")

    return issues
```

**å¤šæ ·æ€§æ£€æŸ¥**ï¼š

```python
def check_tweet_examples_diversity(tweet_examples: List[Dict]) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥ç¤ºä¾‹æ¨æ–‡çš„å¤šæ ·æ€§"""
    issues = []

    # 1. ç±»å‹å¤šæ ·æ€§
    types = [ex.get("type", "") for ex in tweet_examples]
    if len(set(types)) < len(types):
        duplicates = [t for t in set(types) if types.count(t) > 1]
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ content_typeé‡å¤: {duplicates}")

    # 2. å¿ƒæƒ…å¤šæ ·æ€§
    moods = [ex.get("mood", "") for ex in tweet_examples]
    unique_moods = len(set(moods))
    if unique_moods < 4:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ å¿ƒæƒ…å¤šæ ·æ€§ä¸è¶³ (ä»…{unique_moods}ç§moodï¼Œæ¨èè‡³å°‘4ç§)")

    # 3. æ—¶é—´æ®µå¤šæ ·æ€§
    time_segments = [ex.get("time_segment", "") for ex in tweet_examples]
    unique_times = len(set(time_segments))
    if unique_times < 3:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ æ—¶é—´æ®µå¤šæ ·æ€§ä¸è¶³ (ä»…{unique_times}ç§ï¼Œæ¨èè‡³å°‘3ç§)")

    return issues
```

## 9.2 NSFWå†…å®¹è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥

### 9.2.1 è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€æ£€æŸ¥ï¼ˆBODY FIRST, POETRY NEVERï¼‰

è¿™æ˜¯NSFWå†…å®¹æœ€é‡è¦çš„è´¨é‡æ ‡å‡†ã€‚

**ç¦ç”¨è¯æ±‡åº“**ï¼ˆå®Œæ•´åˆ—è¡¨ï¼‰ï¼š

```python
POETIC_FORBIDDEN_WORDS = [
    # æŠ½è±¡æƒ…æ„Ÿ
    "whispers of desire", "echoes of passion", "waves of pleasure",
    "delicate power", "sensual energy", "intimate atmosphere",

    # è¯—æ„åŠ¨è¯
    "bathed in", "dripping with", "curling through", "cascading",
    "shimmering", "pulsing with", "radiating",

    # æŠ½è±¡åè¯
    "ethereal glow", "intimate whispers", "tender exploration",
    "sensual journey", "forbidden pleasure",

    # æ¨¡ç³Šå½¢å®¹è¯
    "delicate", "subtle", "gentle", "soft" (å½“ç”¨äºæè¿°æ€§è¡Œä¸ºæ—¶),

    # éšå–»
    "fire burning", "electricity between", "magnetic pull"
]
```

**æ£€æŸ¥è„šæœ¬**ï¼š
```python
def check_nsfw_content_body_first(text: str) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥NSFWå†…å®¹æ˜¯å¦ç¬¦åˆBODY FIRSTåŸåˆ™"""
    issues = []

    # 1. è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€æ£€æŸ¥
    for phrase in POETIC_FORBIDDEN_WORDS:
        if phrase.lower() in text.lower():
            issues.append(f"âŒ NSFWå†…å®¹åŒ…å«è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€ '{phrase}'")

    # 2. æŠ½è±¡æƒ…æ„Ÿè¯æ£€æŸ¥
    abstract_emotions = ["desire", "passion", "pleasure", "arousal"]
    concrete_indicators = ["touch", "skin", "hand", "finger", "body", "wet", "hard", "ache"]

    has_abstract = any(word in text.lower() for word in abstract_emotions)
    has_concrete = any(word in text.lower() for word in concrete_indicators)

    if has_abstract and not has_concrete:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ NSFWå†…å®¹è¿‡äºæŠ½è±¡ï¼ˆç¼ºå°‘å…·ä½“ç‰©ç†æå†™ï¼‰")

    # 3. æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦æœ‰å…·ä½“èº«ä½“éƒ¨ä½/çŠ¶æ€
    if len(text) > 50:  # ä»…æ£€æŸ¥è¶³å¤Ÿé•¿çš„æ–‡æœ¬
        body_parts_mentioned = sum(1 for word in concrete_indicators if word in text.lower())
        if body_parts_mentioned == 0:
            issues.append("âš ï¸ NSFWå†…å®¹ç¼ºå°‘å…·ä½“èº«ä½“éƒ¨ä½/çŠ¶æ€æå†™")

    return issues
```

**æ­£åç¤ºä¾‹å¯¹æ¯”**ï¼š

| ç±»å‹ | âŒ é”™è¯¯ï¼ˆè¯—æ„ï¼‰ | âœ… æ­£ç¡®ï¼ˆç‰©ç†ï¼‰ |
|------|---------------|----------------|
| **æ¬²æœ›è¡¨è¾¾** | "whispers of desire curling through the quiet" | "can't stop thinking about being bent over that counter" |
| **æ€§å¼ åŠ›** | "the delicate power of submission" | "collar's digging into my throat. hands gripping the edge. waiting" |
| **èº«ä½“æ„Ÿè§‰** | "waves of pleasure washing over her" | "thighs shaking. fingers gripping bedsheet. breathing hard" |
| **æƒ…ç»ªçŠ¶æ€** | "bathed in intimate atmosphere" | "on my knees in front of the mirror. wondering what it'd feel like if someone was here" |

### 9.2.2 Scene Descriptionè´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥

**5è¦ç´ å®Œæ•´æ€§æ£€æŸ¥**ï¼š

```python
def check_scene_description_completeness(scene_hint: str) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥Scene Descriptionçš„5è¦ç´ """
    issues = []

    required_elements = {
        "1_camera_position": {
            "patterns": [r'\b(close-up|full body|medium shot|from above|from below)\b'],
            "examples": "close-up from above, full body shot"
        },
        "2_body_position": {
            "patterns": [r'\b(kneeling|sitting|standing|lying|bent over|on hands and knees)\b'],
            "examples": "kneeling, sitting cross-legged"
        },
        "3_clothing_detail": {
            "patterns": [r'\b(wearing|dressed in|naked|topless|bra|panties|lingerie)\b'],
            "examples": "wearing black lace bra, completely naked"
        },
        "4_exposed_skin": {
            "patterns": [r'\b(exposed|visible|bare|naked|showing|skin)\b'],
            "examples": "bare shoulders, exposed midriff"
        },
        "5_lighting": {
            "patterns": [r'\b(light|lighting|shadow|glow|illuminat|dim|bright)\b'],
            "examples": "soft candlelight, harsh fluorescent"
        }
    }

    for element, config in required_elements.items():
        matched = any(re.search(p, scene_hint, re.IGNORECASE) for p in config["patterns"])
        if not matched:
            issues.append(f"âš ï¸ ç¼ºå°‘ {element.replace('_', ' ')}: {config['examples']}")

    return issues
```

### 9.2.3 Nudityè§„åˆ™æ£€æŸ¥ï¼ˆå…³é”®ï¼‰

è¿™æ˜¯é¿å…ç”Ÿæˆè¿è§„å†…å®¹çš„å…³é”®æ£€æŸ¥ã€‚

**æ£€æŸ¥é€»è¾‘**ï¼š
```python
def check_nudity_rules(scene_hint: str, explicit_nudity_allowed: bool) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥Scene Hintæ˜¯å¦ç¬¦åˆNudityè§„åˆ™"""
    issues = []

    # æ˜¾å¼è£¸éœ²è¯æ±‡
    explicit_body_parts = [
        "nipples", "pussy", "vagina", "genitals", "labia",
        "clitoris", "penis", "dick", "cock", "anus"
    ]

    # éšæ™¦æè¿°ï¼ˆä¹Ÿç®—è¿è§„ï¼‰
    implicit_references = [
        "nipples visible", "nipples erect", "nipples showing",
        "pussy visible", "pussy lips", "between her legs visible",
        "naked pussy", "exposed pussy"
    ]

    scene_lower = scene_hint.lower()

    if not explicit_nudity_allowed:
        # å¦‚æœä¸å…è®¸æ˜¾å¼è£¸éœ²ï¼Œä¸¥æ ¼æ£€æŸ¥
        for word in explicit_body_parts:
            if word in scene_lower:
                issues.append(f"âŒ CRITICAL: explicit_nudity_allowed=Falseæ—¶ä¸èƒ½æåŠ '{word}'")

        for phrase in implicit_references:
            if phrase in scene_lower:
                issues.append(f"âŒ CRITICAL: explicit_nudity_allowed=Falseæ—¶ä¸èƒ½ä½¿ç”¨ '{phrase}'")

        # æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦æ­£ç¡®ä½¿ç”¨"é®ç›–ç‰©"æè¿°
        covering_words = ["covering", "hidden", "concealed", "under", "wearing"]
        has_covering = any(word in scene_lower for word in covering_words)

        if "naked" in scene_lower or "nude" in scene_lower:
            if not has_covering:
                issues.append("âš ï¸ å¦‚æœåŒ…å«'naked/nude'ï¼Œå¿…é¡»è¯´æ˜é®ç›–ç‰©ï¼ˆå¦‚'hands covering chest'ï¼‰")

    else:
        # å¦‚æœå…è®¸æ˜¾å¼è£¸éœ²ï¼Œæ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦è¶³å¤Ÿå…·ä½“
        if any(word in scene_lower for word in ["naked", "nude", "topless"]):
            # å¿…é¡»æœ‰å…·ä½“çš„èº«ä½“éƒ¨ä½æè¿°
            has_explicit_parts = any(word in scene_lower for word in explicit_body_parts)
            if not has_explicit_parts:
                issues.append("âš ï¸ explicit_nudity_allowed=Trueæ—¶ï¼Œå»ºè®®æ˜ç¡®æè¿°exposed body parts")

    return issues
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹æ£€æŸ¥**ï¼š

```python

# âœ… é€šè¿‡ï¼šè™½ç„¶toplessï¼Œä½†æ˜ç¡®è¯´æ˜"hands covering"
```

```python
def check_language_authenticity_config(persona: Dict) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥Language Authenticityé…ç½®"""
    issues = []

    auth = persona.get("data", {}).get("extensions", {}).get("twitter_persona", {}).get("language_authenticity", {})

    if not auth:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ WARNING: ç¼ºå°‘language_authenticityé…ç½®ï¼ˆçœŸå®æ„Ÿä¼šä¸‹é™ï¼‰")
        return issues

    # 1. casual_lowercase_rate
    lowercase_rate = auth.get("casual_lowercase_rate", 0)
    if lowercase_rate == 0:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ casual_lowercase_rate=0ï¼ˆå»ºè®®0.2-0.4ï¼‰")
    elif lowercase_rate > 0.5:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ casual_lowercase_rateè¿‡é«˜ï¼ˆ>0.5å¯èƒ½è¿‡äºéšæ„ï¼‰")

    # 2. omit_final_period
    omit_period = auth.get("omit_final_period", 0)
    if omit_period == 0:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ omit_final_period=0ï¼ˆå»ºè®®0.5-0.7ï¼‰")

    # 3. typo_patterns
    typo_config = auth.get("typo_patterns", {})
    if not typo_config:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ ç¼ºå°‘typo_patternsé…ç½®")
    else:
        base_rate = typo_config.get("base_rate", 0)
        if base_rate == 0:
            issues.append("âš ï¸ typo base_rate=0ï¼ˆå»ºè®®0.08-0.12ï¼‰")
        elif base_rate > 0.2:
            issues.append("âš ï¸ typo base_rateè¿‡é«˜ï¼ˆ>0.2ä¼šæ˜¾å¾—ä¸ä¸“ä¸šï¼‰")

    # 4. filler_wordså’Œslang
    filler_usage = auth.get("filler_words", {}).get("usage_rate", 0)
    slang_usage = auth.get("slang", {}).get("usage_rate", 0)

    if filler_usage == 0 and slang_usage == 0:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ filler_wordså’Œslangéƒ½æœªå¯ç”¨ï¼ˆå£è¯­åŒ–ä¸è¶³ï¼‰")

    return issues
```

**æ¨èé…ç½®èŒƒå›´**ï¼š

### 9.3.2 Strategic Flawsæ£€æŸ¥

**å¿…æ£€é¡¹**ï¼š

```python
def check_strategic_flaws_config(persona: Dict) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥Strategic Flawsé…ç½®"""
    issues = []

    flaws_config = persona.get("data", {}).get("extensions", {}).get("twitter_persona", {}).get("strategic_flaws", {})

    if not flaws_config:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ WARNING: ç¼ºå°‘strategic_flawsé…ç½®ï¼ˆçœŸå®æ„Ÿä¼šä¸‹é™ï¼‰")
        return issues

    active_flaws = flaws_config.get("active_flaws", [])

    # 1. è‡³å°‘å¯ç”¨2ç§flaws
    if len(active_flaws) < 2:
        issues.append("âš ï¸ active_flawså°‘äº2ç§ï¼ˆå»ºè®®2-4ç§ï¼‰")

    # 2. æ£€æŸ¥é¢‘ç‡è®¾ç½®
    flaws = flaws_config.get("flaws", {})
    total_frequency = 0

    for flaw_name in active_flaws:
        if flaw_name not in flaws:
            issues.append(f"âŒ ERROR: active_flawsä¸­çš„'{flaw_name}'æœªå®šä¹‰")
            continue

        freq = flaws[flaw_name].get("frequency", 0)
        total_frequency += freq

        if freq == 0:
            issues.append(f"âš ï¸ '{flaw_name}' frequency=0ï¼ˆè¯¥flawä¸ä¼šè§¦å‘ï¼‰")
        elif freq > 0.3:
            issues.append(f"âš ï¸ '{flaw_name}' frequencyè¿‡é«˜ï¼ˆ>{0.3}ä¼šè¿‡äºé¢‘ç¹ï¼‰")

    # 3. æ€»é¢‘ç‡æ£€æŸ¥
    if total_frequency < 0.15:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ æ€»flawé¢‘ç‡è¿‡ä½ ({total_frequency:.2f}ï¼Œæ¨è0.2-0.3)")
    elif total_frequency > 0.4:
        issues.append(f"âš ï¸ æ€»flawé¢‘ç‡è¿‡é«˜ ({total_frequency:.2f}ï¼Œæ¨è0.2-0.3)")

    return issues
```

### 9.3.3 é¿å…AIæ¨¡å¼æ£€æŸ¥

**ç¦ç”¨æ¨¡å¼åˆ—è¡¨**ï¼š

```python
AI_PATTERNS = {
    "åˆ—è¡¨å¼formatting": [
        r'^\s*[-*â€¢]\s',  # bullet points
        r'^\s*\d+\.\s',  # ç¼–å·åˆ—è¡¨
    ],
    "è¥é”€è¯­è¨€": [
        "excited to share", "link in bio", "check out my",
        "what do you think", "let me know", "tell me in comments",
        "swipe up", "tap the link"
    ],
    "è¿‡åº¦çƒ­æƒ…æ ‡ç‚¹": [
        r'!!!+',  # 3ä¸ªä»¥ä¸Šæ„Ÿå¹å·
        r'ğŸ˜ğŸ˜ğŸ˜',  # é‡å¤emoji 3æ¬¡ä»¥ä¸Š
    ],
    "GenericçŸ­è¯­": [
        "living my best life", "blessed", "grateful for",
        "good vibes only", "positive energy"
    ]
}
```

**æ£€æŸ¥è„šæœ¬**ï¼š
```python
def check_ai_patterns(text: str) -> List[str]:
    """æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«æ˜æ˜¾çš„AIæ¨¡å¼"""
    issues = []

    # 1. åˆ—è¡¨å¼æ£€æŸ¥
    if re.search(AI_PATTERNS["åˆ—è¡¨å¼formatting"][0], text, re.MULTILINE):
        issues.append("âŒ åŒ…å«bullet pointsï¼ˆAIæ¨¡å¼ï¼‰")
    if re.search(AI_PATTERNS["åˆ—è¡¨å¼formatting"][1], text, re.MULTILINE):
        issues.append("âŒ åŒ…å«ç¼–å·åˆ—è¡¨ï¼ˆAIæ¨¡å¼ï¼‰")

    # 2. è¥é”€è¯­è¨€
    for phrase in AI_PATTERNS["è¥é”€è¯­è¨€"]:
        if phrase.lower() in text.lower():
            issues.append(f"âŒ åŒ…å«è¥é”€è¯­è¨€ '{phrase}'ï¼ˆAI/Influenceræ¨¡å¼ï¼‰")

    # 3. è¿‡åº¦çƒ­æƒ…
    if re.search(AI_PATTERNS["è¿‡åº¦çƒ­æƒ…æ ‡ç‚¹"][0], text):
        issues.append("âš ï¸ è¿‡åº¦ä½¿ç”¨æ„Ÿå¹å·ï¼ˆ3+è¿ç»­ï¼‰")

    # 4. GenericçŸ­è¯­
    for phrase in AI_PATTERNS["GenericçŸ­è¯­"]:
        if phrase.lower() in text.lower():
            issues.append(f"âš ï¸ ä½¿ç”¨genericçŸ­è¯­ '{phrase}'ï¼ˆç¼ºä¹ä¸ªæ€§ï¼‰")

    return issues
```

```python
- âœ… ALWAYS use: concrete body parts, physical sensations, specific actions
```

**Step 2ï¼šæ›¿æ¢Few-Shot Examples**

```python
# ä¿®å¤è„šæœ¬
def fix_poetic_language(scene_hint: str) -> str:
    """è‡ªåŠ¨æ›¿æ¢è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€"""
    replacements = {
        "whispers of desire": "aching to be touched",
        "bathed in moonlight": "standing by the window in dim light",
        "delicate power": "control",
        "sensual energy": "sexual tension"
    }

    fixed = scene_hint
    for poetic, concrete in replacements.items():
        fixed = re.sub(poetic, concrete, fixed, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    return fixed
```

### 9.4.2 é—®é¢˜2ï¼šGeneric Detailsï¼ˆç¼ºä¹å…·ä½“æ€§ï¼‰

**ç—‡çŠ¶**ï¼š
- åœ°ç‚¹æè¿°ï¼š"a city in the US"
- å“ç‰Œæè¿°ï¼š"her favorite clothing brand"
- æ—¶é—´æè¿°ï¼š"in the morning"

```python
Generate a complete Character Card V2 persona based on this image.

1. **SPECIFICITY IS MANDATORY**:
   - âŒ NEVER: "a city", "her favorite brand", "morning"
   - âœ… ALWAYS: "Portland, Alberta Arts District", "Free People", "9:30 AM"

2. Use REAL brands: Stumptown, Glossier, Free People, Urban Outfitters

[rest of prompt...]
```

**Step 2ï¼šæé«˜Temperature**

```python
GENERIC_TO_SPECIFIC = {
    "a city in the US": "Portland, Oregon",
    "her favorite coffee shop": "Stumptown on Division St",
    "her favorite clothing brand": "Free People",
    "in the morning": "around 9:30 AM",
    "in the afternoon": "around 2 PM",
    "at night": "around 11 PM"
}

def fix_generic_details(text: str) -> str:
    fixed = text
    for generic, specific in GENERIC_TO_SPECIFIC.items():
        fixed = re.sub(generic, specific, fixed, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
    return fixed
```

### 9.4.3 é—®é¢˜3ï¼šAI Patternsæ˜æ˜¾ï¼ˆåˆ—è¡¨å¼ã€è¥é”€è¯­è¨€ï¼‰

```python
def validate_no_bullet_points(text: str) -> bool:
    """éªŒè¯æ–‡æœ¬ä¸åŒ…å«bullet points"""
    if re.search(r'^\s*[-*â€¢]\s', text, re.MULTILINE):
        return False
    if re.search(r'^\s*\d+\.\s', text, re.MULTILINE):
        return False
    return True

# åœ¨Stage 1ç”Ÿæˆå
if not validate_no_bullet_points(persona["data"]["description"]):
    logger.warning("DescriptionåŒ…å«bullet pointsï¼Œé‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆ...")
    # é‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆé€»è¾‘
```

### 9.4.4 é—®é¢˜4ï¼šScene Hintå¤ªçŸ­æˆ–å¤ªé•¿

**ç—‡çŠ¶**ï¼š
- å¤ªçŸ­ï¼ˆ<50 wordsï¼‰ï¼šç”Ÿæˆå›¾ç‰‡éšæœºæ€§é«˜ï¼Œç»†èŠ‚ä¸å¯æ§
- å¤ªé•¿ï¼ˆ>200 wordsï¼‰ï¼šæ¨¡å‹æ³¨æ„åŠ›åˆ†æ•£ï¼Œå¿½ç•¥ç»†èŠ‚

**ä¿®å¤æ–¹æ¡ˆ**ï¼š

**è‡ªåŠ¨é•¿åº¦è°ƒæ•´**ï¼š
```python
def adjust_scene_hint_length(scene_hint: str, target_min=80, target_max=150) -> str:
    """è‡ªåŠ¨è°ƒæ•´Scene Hinté•¿åº¦"""
    word_count = len(scene_hint.split())

    if word_count < target_min:
        # å¤ªçŸ­ï¼šæ·»åŠ ç»†èŠ‚
        logger.info(f"Scene Hintå¤ªçŸ­ ({word_count} words)ï¼Œæ·»åŠ ç»†èŠ‚...")

        # ä½¿ç”¨LLMæ‰©å†™
        expansion_prompt = f"""
Expand this scene description to {target_min}-{target_max} words by adding:
1. More specific clothing details (fabric, fit, color)
2. Facial expression details (muscle movements, eye direction)
3. Lighting details (color temperature, shadows, direction)
4. Background details (specific objects, textures)

Original ({word_count} words):
{scene_hint}

Expanded version (natural paragraph, {target_min}-{target_max} words):
"""
        expanded = llm_client.generate(expansion_prompt, temperature=0.8)
        return expanded

    elif word_count > target_max:
        # å¤ªé•¿ï¼šå‹ç¼©
        logger.info(f"Scene Hintå¤ªé•¿ ({word_count} words)ï¼Œå‹ç¼©...")

        compression_prompt = f"""
Compress this scene description to {target_max} words while keeping:
1. Camera angle
2. Body position
3. Main clothing items
4. Primary lighting
5. Key facial expression

Remove:
- Redundant adjectives
- Secondary background details
- Repetitive descriptions

Original ({word_count} words):
{scene_hint}

Compressed version ({target_max} words max):
"""
        compressed = llm_client.generate(compression_prompt, temperature=0.7)
        return compressed

    else:
        return scene_hint  # é•¿åº¦åˆé€‚
```

### 9.4.5 é—®é¢˜5ï¼šLoRAæ•ˆæœä¸ç¨³å®šï¼ˆå¤–è²Œæ¼‚ç§»ï¼‰

**ç—‡çŠ¶**ï¼š
- 10å¼ å›¾ç‰‡ä¸­ï¼Œåªæœ‰6-7å¼ æ˜¯"åŒä¸€ä¸ªäºº"
- å‘è‰²ã€è„¸å‹å¶å°”ä¸ä¸€è‡´
- æœ‰æ—¶å®Œå…¨å˜æˆå¦ä¸€ä¸ªäºº

**è¯Šæ–­æ–¹æ³•**ï¼š

```python
def diagnose_lora_instability(persona: Dict, generated_images: List[str]) -> Dict:
    """è¯Šæ–­LoRAä¸ç¨³å®šçš„åŸå› """
    diagnosis = {"issues": [], "recommendations": []}

    lora_config = persona.get("data", {}).get("lora", {})

    # 1. æ£€æŸ¥strengthè®¾ç½®
    strength = lora_config.get("strength", 0)
    if strength < 0.7:
        diagnosis["issues"].append(f"LoRA strengthè¿‡ä½ ({strength})")
        diagnosis["recommendations"].append("æé«˜strengthåˆ°0.8-0.9")

    # 2. æ£€æŸ¥trigger wordä½¿ç”¨
    trigger_words = lora_config.get("trigger_words", [])
    if not trigger_words:
        diagnosis["issues"].append("æœªè®¾ç½®trigger_words")
        diagnosis["recommendations"].append("æ·»åŠ trigger_wordsåˆ°loraé…ç½®")

    # 3. æ£€æŸ¥Scene Hintä¸­æ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«å¤–è²Œæè¿°
    tweet_examples = persona.get("data", {}).get("extensions", {}).get("twitter_persona", {}).get("tweet_examples", [])

    for i, example in enumerate(tweet_examples):
        scene_hint = example.get("scene_hint", "")

        # æ£€æŸ¥å¤–è²Œå†²çª
        appearance_conflicts = ["blonde", "brunette", "black hair", "curvy", "slim", "athletic"]
        for word in appearance_conflicts:
            if word.lower() in scene_hint.lower():
                diagnosis["issues"].append(f"Tweet {i+1} Scene HintåŒ…å«å¤–è²Œæè¿° '{word}'")
                diagnosis["recommendations"].append(f"ä»Scene Hintä¸­åˆ é™¤æ‰€æœ‰å¤–è²Œæè¿°")
                break

    # 4. æ£€æŸ¥CFGè®¾ç½®
    generation_params = persona.get("data", {}).get("extensions", {}).get("twitter_persona", {}).get("generation_params", {})
    cfg = generation_params.get("cfg_scale", 7.0)

    if strength > 0.9 and cfg > 8.0:
        diagnosis["issues"].append(f"LoRA strength ({strength}) + CFG ({cfg}) è¿‡é«˜ï¼Œå¯èƒ½è¿‡æ‹Ÿåˆ")
        diagnosis["recommendations"].append("é™ä½CFGåˆ°7.0æˆ–é™ä½strengthåˆ°0.8")

    return diagnosis
```

**ä¿®å¤æ–¹æ¡ˆ**ï¼š

| åŸå›  | ç—‡çŠ¶ | ä¿®å¤æ–¹æ¡ˆ |
|------|------|---------|
| **Strengthè¿‡ä½** | å¤–è²Œä¸ä¸€è‡´ç‡>30% | æé«˜åˆ°0.8-0.9 |
| **ç¼ºå°‘Trigger Word** | LoRAæ•ˆæœå¼± | åœ¨æ¯ä¸ªScene Hintå¼€å¤´æ·»åŠ trigger |
| **Scene HintåŒ…å«å¤–è²Œæè¿°** | å‘è‰²/è„¸å‹å†²çª | åˆ é™¤æ‰€æœ‰å¤–è²Œç›¸å…³è¯æ±‡ |
| **CFGè¿‡é«˜ + Strengthè¿‡é«˜** | å§¿æ€åƒµç¡¬ã€artifacts | é™ä½CFGåˆ°7.0æˆ–strengthåˆ°0.8 |
| **LoRAæ¨¡å‹è´¨é‡å·®** | æ ¹æœ¬æ— æ³•æ§åˆ¶å¤–è²Œ | é‡æ–°è®­ç»ƒLoRAï¼ˆä½¿ç”¨æ›´å¤šç…§ç‰‡ã€æ›´é«˜stepsï¼‰ |

**é‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆç­–ç•¥**ï¼š
```bash
# å¦‚æœ10å¼ å›¾ç‰‡ä¸­>3å¼ ä¸ä¸€è‡´ï¼Œé‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆ
python main.py \
  --generate-images \
  --tweets-batch output_standalone/problematic_batch.json \
  --lora-strength 0.9  # æé«˜å¼ºåº¦
  --cfg-scale 7.0      # ç¡®ä¿CFGä¸è¿‡é«˜
```

## 9.5 è¿­ä»£ä¼˜åŒ–æµç¨‹

### 9.5.1 ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡ç”Ÿæˆåçš„æ£€æŸ¥æµç¨‹

**å®Œæ•´æ£€æŸ¥Pipeline**ï¼š

```python
def full_quality_check(persona_file: str) -> Dict:
    """å®Œæ•´è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥æµç¨‹"""

    with open(persona_file, 'r') as f:
        persona = json.load(f)

    report = {
        "persona_name": persona.get("data", {}).get("name", "Unknown"),
        "file": persona_file,
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
        "issues": {
            "critical": [],  # å¿…é¡»ä¿®å¤
            "warnings": [],  # å»ºè®®ä¿®å¤
            "info": []       # ä¿¡æ¯æç¤º
        },
        "scores": {}
    }

    # === 1. Stage 1-3æ£€æŸ¥ ===
    print("ğŸ” æ£€æŸ¥Stage 1-3...")

    # System Prompt
    sp_issues = check_system_prompt(persona)
    for issue in sp_issues:
        if "CRITICAL" in issue or "ERROR" in issue:
            report["issues"]["critical"].append(("system_prompt", issue))
        else:
            report["issues"]["warnings"].append(("system_prompt", issue))

    # Description
    desc_issues = check_description(persona)
    for issue in desc_issues:
        if "ERROR" in issue:
            report["issues"]["critical"].append(("description", issue))
        else:
            report["issues"]["warnings"].append(("description", issue))

    # Personality
    pers_issues = check_personality_show_dont_tell(persona.get("data", {}).get("personality", ""))
    for issue in pers_issues:
        report["issues"]["warnings"].append(("personality", issue))

    # Example Tweets
    tweet_examples = persona.get("data", {}).get("extensions", {}).get("twitter_persona", {}).get("tweet_examples", [])

    for i, example in enumerate(tweet_examples):
        scene_hint = example.get("scene_hint", "")
        hint_issues = check_scene_hint_quality(scene_hint)
        for issue in hint_issues:
            if "ERROR" in issue or "CRITICAL" in issue:
                report["issues"]["critical"].append((f"tweet_{i+1}_scene_hint", issue))
            else:
                report["issues"]["warnings"].append((f"tweet_{i+1}_scene_hint", issue))

    # === 2. NSFWå†…å®¹æ£€æŸ¥ ===
    print("ğŸ” æ£€æŸ¥NSFWå†…å®¹...")

    for i, example in enumerate(tweet_examples):
        tweet_text = example.get("text", "")
        scene_hint = example.get("scene_hint", "")

        # è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€æ£€æŸ¥
        nsfw_issues = check_nsfw_content_body_first(tweet_text + " " + scene_hint)
        for issue in nsfw_issues:
            if "ERROR" in issue or "CRITICAL" in issue:
                report["issues"]["critical"].append((f"tweet_{i+1}_nsfw", issue))
            else:
                report["issues"]["warnings"].append((f"tweet_{i+1}_nsfw", issue))

    # === 3. çœŸå®æ„Ÿæ£€æŸ¥ ===
    print("ğŸ” æ£€æŸ¥çœŸå®æ„Ÿé…ç½®...")

    auth_issues = check_language_authenticity_config(persona)
    for issue in auth_issues:
        report["issues"]["warnings"].append(("authenticity", issue))

    flaws_issues = check_strategic_flaws_config(persona)
    for issue in flaws_issues:
        report["issues"]["warnings"].append(("strategic_flaws", issue))

    # === 4. AIæ¨¡å¼æ£€æŸ¥ ===
    print("ğŸ” æ£€æŸ¥AIæ¨¡å¼...")

    ai_pattern_issues = check_ai_patterns(persona.get("data", {}).get("description", ""))
    for issue in ai_pattern_issues:
        if "ERROR" in issue:
            report["issues"]["critical"].append(("ai_patterns", issue))
        else:
            report["issues"]["warnings"].append(("ai_patterns", issue))

    # === 5. è®¡ç®—è´¨é‡åˆ†æ•° ===
    critical_count = len(report["issues"]["critical"])
    warning_count = len(report["issues"]["warnings"])

    # æ»¡åˆ†100ï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªcriticalæ‰£10åˆ†ï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªwarningæ‰£3åˆ†
    score = max(0, 100 - (critical_count * 10) - (warning_count * 3))

    report["scores"]["overall"] = score
    report["scores"]["grade"] = (
        "S" if score >= 95 else
        "A" if score >= 85 else
        "B" if score >= 75 else
        "C" if score >= 65 else
        "D"
    )

    # === 6. ç”ŸæˆæŠ¥å‘Š ===
    print("\n" + "="*70)
    print(f"ğŸ“Š è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥æŠ¥å‘Š: {report['persona_name']}")
    print("="*70)
    print(f"è¯„åˆ†: {score}/100 (ç­‰çº§: {report['scores']['grade']})")
    print(f"Critical Issues: {critical_count}")
    print(f"Warnings: {warning_count}")

    if critical_count > 0:
        print("\nğŸš¨ Critical Issues (å¿…é¡»ä¿®å¤):")
        for field, issue in report["issues"]["critical"]:
            print(f"  [{field}] {issue}")

    if warning_count > 0 and warning_count <= 10:  # åªæ˜¾ç¤ºå‰10ä¸ªwarning
        print("\nâš ï¸ Warnings (å»ºè®®ä¿®å¤):")
        for field, issue in report["issues"]["warnings"][:10]:
            print(f"  [{field}] {issue}")

    # ä¿å­˜æŠ¥å‘Š
    report_file = persona_file.replace(".json", "_quality_report.json")
    with open(report_file, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(report, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

    print(f"\nğŸ“„ è¯¦ç»†æŠ¥å‘Šå·²ä¿å­˜: {report_file}")

    return report
```

**ä½¿ç”¨æ–¹æ³•**ï¼š
```bash
# æ£€æŸ¥å•ä¸ªpersona
python check_quality.py --persona personas/luna_harper.json

# æ‰¹é‡æ£€æŸ¥
python check_quality.py --batch personas/*.json
```

### 9.5.2 é’ˆå¯¹æ€§ä¿®å¤æµç¨‹

**åŸºäºæ£€æŸ¥æŠ¥å‘Šçš„ä¿®å¤å†³ç­–æ ‘**ï¼š

```
æ£€æŸ¥æŠ¥å‘Š â†’ åˆ†æé—®é¢˜ç±»åˆ« â†’ é€‰æ‹©ä¿®å¤æ–¹æ¡ˆ

â”œâ”€ Critical Issues (å¿…é¡»ä¿®å¤)
â”‚  â”œâ”€ å­—æ®µç¼ºå¤± â†’ é‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆæ•´ä¸ªStage
â”‚  â”œâ”€ æ ¼å¼é”™è¯¯ â†’ é‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆæˆ–æ‰‹åŠ¨ä¿®å¤
â”‚  â””â”€ ç¦ç”¨è¯/è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€ â†’ æ‰‹åŠ¨ç¼–è¾‘æˆ–é‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆ
â”‚
â”œâ”€ Warnings (å»ºè®®ä¿®å¤)
â”‚  â”œâ”€ é•¿åº¦ä¸åˆè§„ â†’ è°ƒæ•´temperatureé‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆ
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Genericæè¿° â†’ å¼ºåŒ–Promptä¸­çš„specificityè¦æ±‚
â”‚  â””â”€ çœŸå®æ„Ÿé…ç½®ç¼ºå¤± â†’ æ‰‹åŠ¨æ·»åŠ é…ç½®
â”‚
â””â”€ Grade < B â†’ å»ºè®®å®Œå…¨é‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆ
```

**ä¿®å¤è„šæœ¬ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š

```python
def auto_fix_persona(persona_file: str, quality_report: Dict) -> str:
    """åŸºäºè´¨é‡æŠ¥å‘Šè‡ªåŠ¨ä¿®å¤persona"""

    with open(persona_file, 'r') as f:
        persona = json.load(f)

    fixes_applied = []

    # 1. è‡ªåŠ¨ä¿®å¤ï¼šåˆ é™¤è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€
    for i, example in enumerate(persona.get("data", {}).get("extensions", {}).get("twitter_persona", {}).get("tweet_examples", [])):
        scene_hint = example.get("scene_hint", "")
        original_hint = scene_hint

        # æ›¿æ¢è¯—æ„çŸ­è¯­
        scene_hint = fix_poetic_language(scene_hint)

        if scene_hint != original_hint:
            persona["data"]["extensions"]["twitter_persona"]["tweet_examples"][i]["scene_hint"] = scene_hint
            fixes_applied.append(f"ä¿®å¤tweet_{i+1}çš„è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€")

    # 2. è‡ªåŠ¨ä¿®å¤ï¼šæ·»åŠ Language Authenticityé…ç½®ï¼ˆå¦‚æœç¼ºå¤±ï¼‰
    if "language_authenticity" not in persona.get("data", {}).get("extensions", {}).get("twitter_persona", {}):
        default_auth_config = {
            "casual_lowercase_rate": 0.3,
            "omit_final_period": 0.6,
            "typo_patterns": {
                "base_rate": 0.1,
                "common_typos": [
                    {"from": "can't", "to": "cant", "probability": 0.4},
                    {"from": "you're", "to": "youre", "probability": 0.3}
                ]
            },
            "filler_words": {
                "usage_rate": 0.4,
                "words": ["like", "literally", "tbh", "ngl"]
            },
            "slang": {
                "usage_rate": 0.5,
                "terms": ["vibes", "mood", "fr fr", "no cap"]
            }
        }

        if "twitter_persona" not in persona["data"]["extensions"]:
            persona["data"]["extensions"]["twitter_persona"] = {}

        persona["data"]["extensions"]["twitter_persona"]["language_authenticity"] = default_auth_config
        fixes_applied.append("æ·»åŠ é»˜è®¤Language Authenticityé…ç½®")

    # 3. ä¿å­˜ä¿®å¤åçš„persona
    fixed_file = persona_file.replace(".json", "_fixed.json")
    with open(fixed_file, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(persona, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

    print(f"\nâœ… è‡ªåŠ¨ä¿®å¤å®Œæˆ: {len(fixes_applied)}é¡¹")
    for fix in fixes_applied:
        print(f"  - {fix}")
    print(f"ğŸ“„ ä¿å­˜è‡³: {fixed_file}")

    return fixed_file
```

### 9.5.3 A/Bæµ‹è¯•æµç¨‹

**ç›®çš„**ï¼šå¯¹æ¯”ä¸åŒç‰ˆæœ¬çš„personaè´¨é‡ï¼Œé€‰æ‹©æœ€ä¼˜ç‰ˆæœ¬ã€‚

**æµ‹è¯•æ–¹æ¡ˆ**ï¼š

```python
async def ab_test_persona_variants(
    image_path: str,
    variant_configs: List[Dict],
    tweets_per_variant: int = 5
) -> Dict:
    """A/Bæµ‹è¯•ä¸åŒpersonaé…ç½®"""

    results = []

    for i, config in enumerate(variant_configs):
        print(f"\nğŸ§ª ç”Ÿæˆå˜ä½“ {i+1}/{len(variant_configs)}: {config['name']}")

        # ç”Ÿæˆpersona
        persona = await persona_generator.generate_from_image(
            image_path=image_path,
            temperature=config.get("temperature", 0.85),
            nsfw_level=config.get("nsfw_level", "enabled"),
            custom_instructions=config.get("custom_instructions", "")
        )

        # ä¿å­˜persona
        persona_file = f"personas/variant_{i+1}_{config['name']}.json"
        with open(persona_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(persona, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

        # è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥
        quality_report = full_quality_check(persona_file)

        # ç”Ÿæˆæµ‹è¯•æ¨æ–‡
        calendar = await generate_test_calendar(persona, days=3)
        tweets = await tweet_generator.generate_batch(
            persona=persona,
            calendar=calendar,
            tweets_count=tweets_per_variant,
            temperature=config.get("tweet_temperature", 1.0)
        )

        # è®°å½•ç»“æœ
        results.append({
            "variant_name": config["name"],
            "persona_file": persona_file,
            "quality_score": quality_report["scores"]["overall"],
            "quality_grade": quality_report["scores"]["grade"],
            "critical_issues": len(quality_report["issues"]["critical"]),
            "warnings": len(quality_report["issues"]["warnings"]),
            "tweets": tweets,
            "config": config
        })

    # æ’åºï¼šæŒ‰è´¨é‡åˆ†æ•°é™åº
    results.sort(key=lambda x: x["quality_score"], reverse=True)

    # ç”Ÿæˆå¯¹æ¯”æŠ¥å‘Š
    print("\n" + "="*70)
    print("ğŸ“Š A/Bæµ‹è¯•ç»“æœ")
    print("="*70)

    for i, result in enumerate(results):
        rank_emoji = "ğŸ¥‡" if i == 0 else "ğŸ¥ˆ" if i == 1 else "ğŸ¥‰" if i == 2 else "  "
        print(f"\n{rank_emoji} å˜ä½“ {i+1}: {result['variant_name']}")
        print(f"   è´¨é‡åˆ†æ•°: {result['quality_score']}/100 (ç­‰çº§: {result['quality_grade']})")
        print(f"   Critical: {result['critical_issues']}, Warnings: {result['warnings']}")
        print(f"   é…ç½®: temp={result['config'].get('temperature')}, nsfw={result['config'].get('nsfw_level')}")

    print(f"\nğŸ† æ¨èä½¿ç”¨: {results[0]['variant_name']} ({results[0]['persona_file']})")

    return results
```

**ç¤ºä¾‹ä½¿ç”¨**ï¼š

```python
# æµ‹è¯•3ç§é…ç½®
variants = [
    {
        "name": "conservative",
        "temperature": 0.8,
        "nsfw_level": "moderate",
        "tweet_temperature": 0.95
    },
    {
        "name": "balanced",
        "temperature": 0.85,
        "nsfw_level": "enabled",
        "tweet_temperature": 1.0
    },
    {
        "name": "wild",
        "temperature": 0.95,
        "nsfw_level": "enabled",
        "tweet_temperature": 1.1,
        "custom_instructions": "Extra emphasis on raw, unfiltered content"
    }
]

results = await ab_test_persona_variants(
    image_path="character_photos/test.png",
    variant_configs=variants,
    tweets_per_variant=5
)
```

## å°ç»“

æœ¬ç« å»ºç«‹äº†å®Œæ•´çš„è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥ä¸ä¼˜åŒ–ä½“ç³»ï¼š

**è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥æ¸…å•**ï¼š
- **Stage 1-3æ£€æŸ¥**ï¼šSystem Promptï¼ˆ200-300å­—ã€4æ®µå¼ï¼‰ã€Descriptionï¼ˆ150-250å­—ã€è‡ªç„¶æ®µè½ï¼‰ã€Personalityï¼ˆShow Don't Tellï¼‰ã€Example Tweetsï¼ˆ8æ¡ã€80-150å­—scene_hintï¼‰
- **NSFWå†…å®¹æ£€æŸ¥**ï¼šç¦ç”¨è¯—æ„è¯­è¨€ã€5è¦ç´ å®Œæ•´æ€§ã€Nudityè§„åˆ™ä¸¥æ ¼æ‰§è¡Œ
- **çœŸå®æ„Ÿæ£€æŸ¥**ï¼šLanguage Authenticityé…ç½®ï¼ˆlowercase 0.2-0.4ã€typo 0.08-0.12ï¼‰ã€Strategic Flawsï¼ˆ2-4ç§ã€æ€»é¢‘ç‡0.2-0.3ï¼‰ã€é¿å…AIæ¨¡å¼

**å¸¸è§é—®é¢˜ä¿®å¤**ï¼š
1. **Poetic Language**ï¼šå¼ºåŒ–System Promptã€æ›¿æ¢Few-Shotã€æ‰‹åŠ¨ç¼–è¾‘
2. **Generic Details**ï¼šè¦æ±‚SPECIFICã€æé«˜temperatureã€æ‰¹é‡æ›¿æ¢
3. **AI Patterns**ï¼šæ ¼å¼éªŒè¯ã€å¼ºåŒ–Anti-Influencerè§„åˆ™
4. **Scene Hinté•¿åº¦**ï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨æ‰©å†™/å‹ç¼©åˆ°80-150å­—
5. **LoRAä¸ç¨³å®š**ï¼šæé«˜strengthã€åˆ é™¤å¤–è²Œæè¿°ã€è°ƒæ•´CFG

**è¿­ä»£ä¼˜åŒ–æµç¨‹**ï¼š
1. **ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡ç”Ÿæˆ**ï¼šå®Œæ•´è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥ï¼ˆè‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–è„šæœ¬ï¼‰
2. **é’ˆå¯¹æ€§ä¿®å¤**ï¼šåŸºäºæŠ¥å‘Šé€‰æ‹©ä¿®å¤æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼ˆå†³ç­–æ ‘ï¼‰
3. **A/Bæµ‹è¯•**ï¼šå¯¹æ¯”å¤šä¸ªå˜ä½“ï¼Œé€‰æ‹©æœ€ä¼˜é…ç½®

**å…³é”®æ´å¯Ÿ**ï¼š
- è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥å¿…é¡»è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–ï¼ˆå‡å°‘äººå·¥æˆæœ¬ï¼‰
- Critical Issueså¿…é¡»100%ä¿®å¤ï¼ˆå¦åˆ™å½±å“ç”Ÿäº§ï¼‰
- A/Bæµ‹è¯•æ˜¯æŒç»­ä¼˜åŒ–çš„æ ¸å¿ƒï¼ˆæ•°æ®é©±åŠ¨ï¼‰
- è´¨é‡åˆ†æ•°Sçº§æ ‡å‡†ï¼š95+åˆ†ã€0 criticalã€<5 warnings

**ä¸‹ä¸€ç« é¢„å‘Š**ï¼šç¬¬åç« å°†æä¾›å®Œæ•´çš„å®æˆ˜æ¡ˆä¾‹ä¸æ¨¡æ¿åº“ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬è½»åº¦/é‡åº¦NSFWäººè®¾å®Œæ•´ç¤ºä¾‹ã€System Promptæ¨¡æ¿ã€Content Type Distributionæ¨¡æ¿ã€Scene Hintæ¨¡æ¿åº“ã€ä»¥åŠå¿«é€Ÿå‚è€ƒè¡¨ã€‚
